## 4. Errors and Fixes

### **Error 1: Background routing was a stub**
- **Symptom**: `ROUTER_BACKGROUND` config was parsed but never fired
- **Root cause**: `_is_background_request()` function didn't exist; no detection logic in `ModelRouter.route()`
- **Fix**: Added `_is_background_request()` function in `model_router.py` that detects haiku family via `_original_model` or low `max_tokens`. Added background routing to priority list before default.
- **How it was discovered**: Audit phase — I verified each routing path and found background missing from the detection chain.

### **Error 2: `.envrc` missing ROUTER_* exports**
- **Symptom**: Shell sessions using direnv wouldn't get `ROUTER_*` variables even though they were in `.env`
- **Root cause**: `.envrc` file (used by direnv for live reloading) didn't export the router config variables that were added to `.env`
- **Fix**: Added all `ROUTER_DEFAULT`, `ROUTER_BACKGROUND`, `ROUTER_THINK`, `ROUTER_LONG_CONTEXT`, `ROUTER_LONG_CONTEXT_THRESHOLD`, `ROUTER_WEB_SEARCH`, `ROUTER_IMAGE`, `ROUTER_CUSTOM_PATH` exports to `.envrc`
- **How it was discovered**: Audit phase after smoke testing config load

### **Error 3: Streaming cascade missing circuit breaker skip**
- **Symptom**: Non-streaming cascade skipped OPEN breakers (line 648-653) but streaming cascade didn't
- **Root cause**: Feature was implemented for non-streaming but not propagated to streaming variant
- **Fix**: Added circuit breaker skip check in streaming cascade (line 1001-1008) that checks `_cb.is_open` and skips to next model if true
- **How it was discovered**: During implementation of recommendation 1 (CB filtering), I reviewed the streaming cascade and found the gap

### **Error 4: Harmful recommendation in council output**
- **Symptom**: Council recommended adding `preferred_max_latency: {p90: 5}` to OR provider object
- **Root cause**: Council misunderstood that this is a hint-only filter, not a hard requirement. At `p90: 5` seconds, it would eliminate endpoints with 8-15s cold-start TTFT
- **Fix**: Decision (not an implementation error) — I recommended persistence instead. Noted in summary that the user should drop the latency filter recommendation if they encounter it.
- **User feedback**: None explicitly on this, but the council identified it as harmful

---

## 5. Problem Solving

**Solved Problems**:
1. **Cascade → circuit breaker feedback gap**: Implemented `_build_or_models_list()` to filter OPEN breakers from OR native injection, preventing wasted routing budget on known-dead models
2. **Soft response failures invisible to circuit breaker**: Implemented `record_parse_ok()` and `record_stream_finish()` to detect structurally broken HTTP 200 responses and penalize models at 0.5 severity
3. **Background routing failures are hard errors**: Implemented `_use_case_tier` fallback mechanism so background model failure triggers cascade instead of failing the request
4. **Circuit breaker state reset on every restart**: Implemented JSON persistence with `from_persist_dict()` cooldown recalculation so OPEN breakers remain OPEN across restarts
5. **Streaming cascade asymmetry**: Added missing circuit breaker skip to streaming variant to match non-streaming behavior

**Verification Performed**:
- Smoke test of all four features: CB filtering, parse_ok tracking, persistence round-trip — all passed
- Manual code review of both streaming and non-streaming paths to ensure parity
- CHANGELOG update documenting all five changes

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - Circuit Breaker Pattern (CLOSED → OPEN → HALF_OPEN state machine with soft/hard failure tracking)
   - OpenRouter Native Fallback (models array + throughput sorting for endpoint selection)
   - Cascade with Exponential Backoff (sequential model fallback on provider errors)
   - Per-Use-Case Model Routing (background, think, long_context, web_search, image detection)
   - RTK (Rust Token Killer) - CLI wrapper for compressing terminal output, NOT a proxy/daemon

   - Proxy Chain - ordered list of upstream services with enable/disable toggles
   - Soft vs Hard Failures - HTTP 200 with broken output (empty content, missing tool_calls, truncated) penalized at 0.5 severity
   - Circuit Breaker Persistence - state saved to data/circuit_breaker_state.json with cooldown recalculation on restore
   - Streaming vs Non-Streaming Cascade parity

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:

**Session 2 (latest, in-progress):**
The user's most recent message asks for:
1. Confirm RTK + Headroom work together; clarify RTK's role (it IS a CLI wrapper, NOT a proxy layer)
2. List ALL configurable "knobs" for both RTK and Headroom, with effects and syntax
3. Make `proxies` command handle ALL proxy chain management: settings, reordering, adding/removing proxies, configuration
4. Recommend models for each task-based substitution slot (free models only, based on scoring data)
5. Describe ideal model characteristics per slot (cheap+fast for tools, large-context for high-token routing, etc.)
6. Enable toggling task substitutions on/off — must work with Anthropic Pro subscription passthrough
7. Set task substitutions via env file AND proxies command
8. Comprehensive metrics: compression stats, tokens in/out per model per date, tool call success rates, web search routing analysis
9. Terminal status bars: static bars in tmux panes for headroom stats, proxy stats, and RTK stats (with color)
10. Claude Code status bar integration: tokens/s, total tokens, tool call success/fail, compression %, tokens saved, proxy health indicators, last error code
11. Fix status bar layout for variable-length model names (left-align some items, right-align others)
12. Create todo list, implement everything, update docs

2. Key Technical Concepts:
- **RTK (Rust Token Killer)** — CLI wrapper (NOT a proxy/daemon) that compresses terminal command output. Runs on-demand via `rtk <command>` prefix. Has 50+ subcommands for different tools. `rtk gain` shows savings. Config via `rtk config --create`. Ultra-compact mode available. No port, no health check.
- **Headroom** — HTTP proxy at :8787 that compresses LLM context/prompts. Multiple optimization modes: `token_headroom` (compress for session extension) vs `cost_savings` (preserve prefix cache). Has knobs for AST-based code compression, intelligent context management, semantic caching, Read lifecycle, and memory. `headroom perf` analyzes compression effectiveness.
- **Proxy Chain** — Ordered list in `config/proxy_chain.json`. Flow: Client → Proxy(:8082) → Headroom(:8787) → OpenRouter. Each entry has id, name, url, port, type (http|cli_wrapper), enabled flag.
- **Circuit Breaker Pattern** — CLOSED→OPEN→HALF_OPEN state machine per model. Soft failures (empty content, missing tool_calls) at 0.5 severity. State persisted to `data/circuit_breaker_state.json`.
- **Model Router** — Per-use-case routing: default, background, think, long_context, web_search, image, custom. Configured via ROUTER_* env vars or proxy_chain.json router section. Custom Python/JS router scripts supported.
- **Cascade Fallback** — Sequential model fallback on provider errors. Dual method: `cascade` (proxy-level retry) + `openrouter_native` (inject models[] array). Circuit breaker filtering on OR models array.
- **Output Token Capping** — New feature: caps max_tokens to model's actual output limit to prevent context overflow (e.g., minimax-m2.5 gets capped to 16384 instead of 128K)
- **direnv + dotenv interaction** — `dotenv.load_dotenv(override=False)` means shell env wins over .env file. Must re-source .envrc after edits for proxy to pick up changes.

3. Files and Code Sections:

- **config/proxy_chain.json**
  - Central chain configuration with entries array and router object
  - Changed `router.background` from `stepfun/step-3.5-flash:free` to `nvidia/nemotron-nano-9b-v2:free`
  - Router section: `{"default":"", "background":"nvidia/nemotron-nano-9b-v2:free", "think":"", "long_context":"minimax/minimax-m2.5:free", "long_context_threshold":60000, "web_search":"", "image":"qwen/qwen2.5-vl-72b-instruct", "custom_router_path":""}`

  - Cascade: `BIG_CASCADE=qwen/qwen3-235b-a22b:free,openai/gpt-oss-120b:free,minimax/minimax-m2.5:free`

- **src/services/conversion/request_converter.py**
  - Added output token capping after model routing:
    ```python
    from src.services.usage.model_limits import get_output_limit
    model_output_limit = get_output_limit(openai_model)
    effective_max = min(config.max_tokens_limit, model_output_limit)
    token_limit = min(
        max(claude_request.max_tokens, config.min_tokens_limit),
        effective_max,
    )
    if token_limit < claude_request.max_tokens:
        logger.debug(
            f"Capped max_tokens {claude_request.max_tokens} → {token_limit} "
            f"(model {openai_model} output limit: {model_output_limit})"
        )
    ```

- **Context overflow on minimax-m2.5 (228K > 196K):**

  - BIG_MODEL=gemini-3.1-pro-high only works with CLIProxyAPI (disabled)
  - Fixed by changing to OpenRouter free models

- **114 models with `output: None` in model_limits.json:**
  - Caused silent fallback to 4096 output limit
  - Fixed via Python script setting reasonable defaults

- **Streaming `stream` parameter duplication:**
  - `openai_endpoints.py` line 350 passed `stream=True` as both dict key and kwarg
  - Error: `got multiple values for keyword argument 'stream'`
  - Fixed by adding `openai_request.pop("stream", None)` before the create() call

- **Proxy process retaining old env vars after .envrc edits:**
  - `dotenv.load_dotenv(override=False)` means shell env wins over .env
  - Process started with old shell env still had `ROUTER_BACKGROUND=stepfun/step-3.5-flash:free`
  - Fixed by killing old process and re-sourcing `.envrc` before starting new process

- **`pkill` returning exit code 144:**
  - Signal-related exit code in bash, had to use `kill <PID>` directly instead

- **nemotron-nano-9b-v2 returning content=None:**
  - Model behavior issue (returns empty content with finish_reason=length on short prompts)
  - Not a proxy bug — model quirk with very short prompts

- Model limits gaps — all active free models now have correct context/output limits
- Streaming parameter duplication — clean separation of dict and kwarg params

**Headroom knobs discovered:**
- `--mode cost_savings|token_headroom` (env: HEADROOM_MODE)
- `--no-optimize` (passthrough mode)
- `--no-cache` (disable semantic caching)
- `--no-code-aware` (disable AST-based code compression)
- `--no-read-lifecycle` (disable stale/superseded Read compression)
- `--no-intelligent-context` (fall back to RollingWindow)
- `--no-intelligent-scoring` (use position-based scoring)
- `--no-compress-first` (disable deep compression before dropping)
- `--budget FLOAT` (daily budget limit)
- `--memory` (persistent user memory)
- `--learn` (live traffic learning)
- `--backend` (anthropic, bedrock, openrouter, anyllm, litellm-*)
- `--openai-api-url`, `--anthropic-api-url`, `--gemini-api-url`

**RTK knobs discovered:**
- `--ultra-compact` / `-u` (Level 2 optimizations)
- `--verbose` / `-v` (verbosity levels)
- `rtk config --create` (creates default config file — likely TOML)
- `rtk trust` / `rtk untrust` (project-local TOML filters)
- Per-command compression (each of 50+ subcommands has its own filter)
- `rtk gain --format json` (machine-readable savings data)

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - RTK (Rust Token Killer): CLI wrapper, no proxy, no port, compresses command output
   - Headroom: HTTP proxy at :8787, compresses LLM context/prompts
   - Proxy Chain: ordered config in proxy_chain.json with entries + router section
   - RouterConfig: dataclass with per-use-case routing (default, background, think, long_context, web_search, image)
   - Circuit Breaker: OPEN/CLOSED/HALF_OPEN per-model state machine
   - Cascade fallback: dual method (proxy-level + OpenRouter native `models[]` array)
   - Passthrough mode: bypass routing + cascade for Anthropic Pro direct use
   - tmux pane-border-status + status-left/right for session status bars
   - Claude Code status line: script outputs to ~/.claude/status-line.sh
   - Stream parameter handling: avoid duplicate `stream` kwarg in openai client

The cmd_help function outputs structured sections: USAGE, LIFECYCLE, MONITORING, CONFIGURATION, CONFIG subcommands, ROUTER subcommands, METRICS subcommands, FILES, EXAMPLES.

   - `/home/cheta/code/claude-code-proxy/src/core/proxy_chain.py` — Added `disabled: bool = False` and `passthrough: bool = False` to RouterConfig. Updated from_dict() parser:
     ```python
     parsed_router_data = {}
     if router_data.get("_disabled"):
         parsed_router_data["disabled"] = True
     if router_data.get("_passthrough"):
         parsed_router_data["passthrough"] = True
     for k, v in router_data.items():
         if k.startswith("_"):
             continue  # Already handled above
         if not hasattr(RouterConfig, k):
             continue
         if k in ["default", "background", "think", "long_context", "web_search", "image"]:
             parsed_router_data[k] = RouteTarget.from_any(v)
         else:
             parsed_router_data[k] = v
     ```

- **Cross-tool cold-start coverage**: How cold-start mitigation applies to Qwen Code, OpenCode, Hermes, OpenClaw; whether we can use their native routing (OpenCode's "Zen"/`openrouter/auto`) with Claude Code and Hermes
- **RTK visibility fix**: RTK not appearing in `proxies status` output at all
- **Hermes routing fix**: How to use the proxy with Hermes
- **Four issues in one message**: RTK absent from proxy terminal pane, mouse scroll producing escape codes (`^[[A^[[B`), where is proxy chain order logic, web UI at :8082 not working for chain management
- **Web UI chain page**: Build a frontend page for proxy chain and router config management (confirmed with "yes")

---

2. Key Technical Concepts:

- **Cold-start two-layer mitigation**: (1) OpenRouter native — injects `models` array + `provider: {sort: {by: throughput}}` so OR races endpoints in parallel; (2) Proxy cascade — sequential fallback with exponential backoff, circuit breaker filtering, Alibaba ramp-up detection
- **Circuit breaker filtering in OR injection**: `_build_or_models_list()` removes OPEN breakers from `models` array before injection
- **Task-based model routing**: `ROUTER_*` env vars (`ROUTER_BACKGROUND`, `ROUTER_IMAGE`, `ROUTER_THINK`, `ROUTER_LONG_CONTEXT`, `ROUTER_WEB_SEARCH`, `ROUTER_DEFAULT`, `ROUTER_CUSTOM_PATH`) override tier models per request type
- **Routing trigger detection**: image blocks → vision model, tool names containing web_search/brave/exa → web_search model, token estimate > threshold → long_context model, `thinking.type=enabled` or "plan mode" in system → think model, haiku family `_original_model` or `max_tokens ≤ 256` → background model
- **RTK (Rust Token Killer)**: CLI wrapper only, NO server mode, NO port. Wraps shell commands to compress output. Integration via CLAUDE.md instructions. `rtk hook` supports Gemini and Copilot formats but NOT Claude Code hooks natively.
- **Headroom**: HTTP context-compression proxy at :8787. Intercepts API requests, compresses message history. Separate from RTK — parallel layers, not sequential.
- **Proxy chain topology**: `Client → Headroom :8787 → Claude Code Proxy :8082 → OpenRouter`. RTK is a side-channel for CLI output, not in the HTTP chain.
- **CLIProxyAPI :8317**: Currently disabled in proxy_chain.json. The intended "port after Headroom" slot.
- **tmux mouse mode**: Was `off`, causing scroll events to pass as cursor key sequences (`^[[A^[[B`)
- **SvelteKit 5**: Web UI uses `$state` runes (not `let` + reactive), Lucide Svelte icons, CSS custom properties for theming (3 themes: Midnight Aurora, Ember Console, Synthwave Minimal)
- **Web UI backend APIs**: `GET/PUT /api/proxy-chain` and `GET/PUT /api/router-config` in `src/api/web_ui.py` — already implemented, hot-reloads running singleton on save
- **Hermes config**: Goes direct to OpenRouter at `https://openrouter.ai/api/v1` — bypasses proxy entirely, missing cold-start protection

---

● Bash(cat scripts/draft-remaining-free.sh)
  ⎿  #!/usr/bin/env bash
     set -euo pipefail

     SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
     REPO_ROOT="$(cd "${SCRIPT_DIR}/.." && pwd)"
     cd "${REPO_ROOT}"

     MAX_RETRIES="${MAX_RETRIES:-4}"
     BACKOFF_BASE_SECONDS="${BACKOFF_BASE_SECONDS:-20}"
     AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS="${AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS:-5500}"
     AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_WORDS="${AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_WORDS:-3200}"
     AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_DELAY_SECONDS="${AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_DELAY_SECONDS:-15}"

     infer_total_chapters() {
       python3 - <<'PY'
     import re
     from pathlib import Path
     text = Path('outline.md').read_text(encoding='utf-8')
     matches = re.findall(r'###\s+\*\*Ch\s+(\d+):|###\s+Ch\s+(\d+):', text)
     nums = [int(a or b) for a, b in matches if a or b]
     print(max(nums) if nums else 18)
     PY
     }

     current_max_chapter() {
       python3 - <<'PY'
     import re
     from pathlib import Path
     nums = []
     for path in Path('chapters').glob('ch_*.md'):
         m = re.search(r'ch_(\d+)\.md$', path.name)
         if m:
             nums.append(int(m.group(1)))
     print(max(nums) if nums else 0)
     PY
     }

     update_state() {
       python3 - <<'PY'
     import json
     from pathlib import Path
     state_path = Path('state.json')
     chapters = sorted(Path('chapters').glob('ch_*.md'))
     count = len(chapters)
     state = {}
     if state_path.exists():
         state = json.loads(state_path.read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
     state['chapters_drafted'] = count
     state['chapters_total'] = max(state.get('chapters_total', 0), count)
     if count >= state.get('chapters_total', count):
         state['phase'] = 'revision'
         state['current_focus'] = 'full_draft_complete'
     else:
         state['phase'] = 'drafting'
         state['current_focus'] = f'chapter_{count + 1:02d}'
     state_path.write_text(json.dumps(state, indent=2), encoding='utf-8')
     PY
     }

     TOTAL_CHAPTERS="${TOTAL_CHAPTERS:-$(infer_total_chapters)}"
     START_CHAPTER="${START_CHAPTER:-$(( $(current_max_chapter) + 1 ))}"

     printf '[draft-loop] total_chapters=%s\n' "$TOTAL_CHAPTERS" >&2
     printf '[draft-loop] start_chapter=%s\n' "$START_CHAPTER" >&2
     printf '[draft-loop] max_output=%s\n' "$AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS" >&2

     if (( START_CHAPTER > TOTAL_CHAPTERS )); then
       echo "[draft-loop] Nothing to do." >&2
       update_state
       exit 0
     fi

     for (( chapter=START_CHAPTER; chapter<=TOTAL_CHAPTERS; chapter++ )); do
       printf '\n[draft-loop] chapter=%02d\n' "$chapter" >&2
       success=0
       for (( attempt=1; attempt<=MAX_RETRIES; attempt++ )); do
         printf '[draft-loop] attempt=%s/%s chapter=%02d\n' "$attempt" "$MAX_RETRIES" "$chapter" >&2
         if /usr/bin/time -f '[draft-loop] elapsed=%E exit=%x' \
           env \
             AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS="$AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS" \
             AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_WORDS="$AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_WORDS" \
             AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_DELAY_SECONDS="$AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_DELAY_SECONDS" \
             "${SCRIPT_DIR}/run-openrouter-hybrid.sh" draft_chapter.py "$chapter"
         then
           success=1
           update_state
           break
         fi
         wait_seconds=$(( BACKOFF_BASE_SECONDS * attempt ))
         printf '[draft-loop] chapter=%02d failed, backing off %ss\n' "$chapter" "$wait_seconds" >&2
         sleep "$wait_seconds"
       done
       if (( success == 0 )); then
         printf '[draft-loop] chapter=%02d failed after %s attempts\n' "$chapter" "$MAX_RETRIES" >&2
         exit 1
       fi
     done

     update_state
     echo "[draft-loop] completed all chapters" >&2

● Bash(cat scripts/run-openrouter-hybrid.sh)
  ⎿  #!/usr/bin/env bash
     set -euo pipefail

     SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
     REPO_ROOT="$(cd "${SCRIPT_DIR}/.." && pwd)"
     cd "${REPO_ROOT}"

     API_KEY="${OPENROUTER_API_KEY:-${ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN:-}}"

     if [[ -z "${API_KEY}" ]]; then
       echo "ERROR: set OPENROUTER_API_KEY (or ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN) first." >&2
       exit 1
     fi

     export AUTONOVEL_API_MODE=claude_code
     export ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL="${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL:-https://openrouter.ai/api}"
     export ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN="${ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN:-${API_KEY}}"
     export ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=""
     export AUTONOVEL_API_KEY=""
     export AUTONOVEL_AUTH_TOKEN=""

     export AUTONOVEL_WRITER_MODEL="${AUTONOVEL_WRITER_MODEL:-stepfun/step-3.5-flash:free}"
     export AUTONOVEL_JUDGE_MODEL="${AUTONOVEL_JUDGE_MODEL:-z-ai/glm-5}"
     export AUTONOVEL_REVIEW_MODEL="${AUTONOVEL_REVIEW_MODEL:-arcee-ai/trinity-large-preview:free}"

     export AUTONOVEL_ENABLE_GIT="${AUTONOVEL_ENABLE_GIT:-0}"
     export AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS="${AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS:-4000}"

     echo "[openrouter-hybrid] base=${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL}" >&2
     echo "[openrouter-hybrid] writer=${AUTONOVEL_WRITER_MODEL}" >&2
     echo "[openrouter-hybrid] judge=${AUTONOVEL_JUDGE_MODEL}" >&2
     echo "[openrouter-hybrid] review=${AUTONOVEL_REVIEW_MODEL}" >&2
     echo "[openrouter-hybrid] max_output=${AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS}" >&2

     exec uv run python "$@"

● Bash(cat scripts/launch-agent.sh)
  ⎿  #!/usr/bin/env bash
     set -euo pipefail

     SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
     REPO_ROOT="$(cd "${SCRIPT_DIR}/.." && pwd)"

     if [[ -f "${REPO_ROOT}/.agent-launcher.env" ]]; then
       # shellcheck disable=SC1091
       source "${REPO_ROOT}/.agent-launcher.env"
     fi

     usage() {
       cat <<'EOF'
     Usage: scripts/launch-agent.sh <agent> [args...]

     Agents:
       claude     Claude Code / Anthropic-compatible gateway
       codex      OpenAI Codex CLI
       opencode   OpenCode CLI
       qwen       Qwen Code CLI
       gemini     Gemini CLI
       custom     User-defined command via CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN

     Core env vars:
       AGENT_ROUTE=native|proxy|openrouter       Default: native
       AGENT_MODE=default|acp                    Default: default
       AGENT_EDITOR="code --wait"                Exported as EDITOR when set

     Proxy/OpenRouter env vars:
       AGENT_PROXY_URL=http://localhost:8082
       AGENT_OPENAI_PROXY_URL=http://localhost:8082/v1
       AGENT_PROXY_KEY=pass
       OPENROUTER_API_KEY=...

     Custom agent env vars:
       CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN=/path/to/binary
       CUSTOM_AGENT_ARGS="--flag value"
       CUSTOM_AGENT_ACP_ARGS="--acp"

     Examples (WSL/bash):
       scripts/launch-agent.sh claude --continue --dangerously-skip-permissions --verbose --model=opus
       AGENT_ROUTE=proxy scripts/launch-agent.sh claude --continue --model=opus
       AGENT_ROUTE=openrouter OPENAI_MODEL=gpt-5.2-codex scripts/launch-agent.sh codex
       AGENT_MODE=acp scripts/launch-agent.sh qwen
       AGENT_MODE=acp scripts/launch-agent.sh opencode
     EOF
     }

     log() {
       printf '[launch-agent] %s\n' "$*" >&2
     }

     require_cmd() {
       if ! command -v "$1" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
         log "Missing required command: $1"
         exit 1
       fi
     }

     split_args() {
       local raw="${1:-}"
       SPLIT_RESULT=()
       if [[ -z "${raw}" ]]; then
         return 0
       fi
       # Intentional word splitting for user-supplied launcher args.
       # shellcheck disable=SC2206
       SPLIT_RESULT=( ${raw} )
     }

     set_editor_env() {
       if [[ -n "${AGENT_EDITOR:-}" ]]; then
         export EDITOR="${AGENT_EDITOR}"
       fi
     }

     setup_claude_env() {
       local route="${AGENT_ROUTE:-native}"
       case "${route}" in
         native)
           ;;
         proxy)
           export ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL="${AGENT_PROXY_URL:-http://localhost:8082}"
           export ANTHROPIC_API_KEY="${AGENT_PROXY_KEY:-pass}"
           export CLAUDE_CODE_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS="${CLAUDE_CODE_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS:-128768}"
           ;;
         openrouter)
           : "${OPENROUTER_API_KEY:?Set OPENROUTER_API_KEY for AGENT_ROUTE=openrouter}"
           export ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL="${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL:-https://openrouter.ai/api}"
           export ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN="${ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN:-${OPENROUTER_API_KEY}}"
           export ANTHROPIC_API_KEY="${ANTHROPIC_API_KEY:-}"
           ;;
         *)
           log "Unsupported AGENT_ROUTE for claude: ${route}"
           exit 1
           ;;
       esac
     }

     setup_openai_compat_env() {
       local route="${AGENT_ROUTE:-native}"
       case "${route}" in
         native)
           ;;
         proxy)
           export
     OPENAI_BASE_URL="${OPENAI_BASE_URL:-${AGENT_OPENAI_PROXY_URL:-${AGENT_PROXY_URL:-http://localhost:8082}/v1}}"
           export OPENAI_API_KEY="${OPENAI_API_KEY:-${AGENT_PROXY_KEY:-pass}}"
           ;;
         openrouter)
           : "${OPENROUTER_API_KEY:?Set OPENROUTER_API_KEY for AGENT_ROUTE=openrouter}"
           export OPENAI_BASE_URL="${OPENAI_BASE_URL:-https://openrouter.ai/api/v1}"
           export OPENAI_API_KEY="${OPENAI_API_KEY:-${OPENROUTER_API_KEY}}"
           ;;
         *)
           log "Unsupported AGENT_ROUTE for OpenAI-compatible CLI: ${route}"
           exit 1
           ;;
       esac
     }

     setup_opencode_env() {
       local route="${AGENT_ROUTE:-native}"
       case "${route}" in
         native)
           ;;
         proxy)
           export ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL="${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL:-${AGENT_PROXY_URL:-http://localhost:8082}}"
           export ANTHROPIC_API_KEY="${ANTHROPIC_API_KEY:-${AGENT_PROXY_KEY:-pass}}"
           export OPENCODE_EXPERIMENTAL_OUTPUT_TOKEN_MAX="${OPENCODE_EXPERIMENTAL_OUTPUT_TOKEN_MAX:-128768}"
           export OPENCODE_CONFIG_CONTENT="${OPENCODE_CONFIG_CONTENT:-{\"provider\":{\"anthropic\":{\"options\":{\"baseU
     RL\":\"${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL}/v1\"}}}}}"
           ;;
         openrouter)
           : "${OPENROUTER_API_KEY:?Set OPENROUTER_API_KEY for AGENT_ROUTE=openrouter}"
           export ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN="${ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN:-${OPENROUTER_API_KEY}}"
           export ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL="${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL:-https://openrouter.ai/api}"
           export OPENCODE_CONFIG_CONTENT="${OPENCODE_CONFIG_CONTENT:-{\"provider\":{\"anthropic\":{\"options\":{\"baseU
     RL\":\"${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL}/v1\"}}}}}"
           ;;
         *)
           log "Unsupported AGENT_ROUTE for opencode: ${route}"
           exit 1
           ;;
       esac
     }

     setup_gemini_env() {
       local route="${AGENT_ROUTE:-native}"
       if [[ "${route}" != "native" ]]; then
         log "Gemini CLI does not expose a documented generic custom-base-URL mode; use native Google auth."
         exit 1
       fi
     }

     main() {
       if [[ $# -lt 1 ]]; then
         usage
         exit 1
       fi

       local agent="$1"
       shift

       if [[ "${agent}" == "-h" || "${agent}" == "--help" ]]; then
         usage
         exit 0
       fi

       set_editor_env
       cd "${REPO_ROOT}"

       case "${agent}" in
         claude)
           require_cmd claude
           setup_claude_env
           exec claude "$@"
           ;;
         codex)
           require_cmd codex
           if [[ "${AGENT_MODE:-default}" != "default" ]]; then
             log "Codex ACP/IDE server mode is not wired here; use Codex's own IDE integration/config."
             exit 1
           fi
           setup_openai_compat_env
           exec codex "$@"
           ;;
         opencode)
           require_cmd opencode
           setup_opencode_env
           if [[ "${AGENT_MODE:-default}" == "acp" ]]; then
             exec opencode acp "$@"
           fi
           exec opencode "$@"
           ;;
         qwen)
           require_cmd qwen
           setup_openai_compat_env
           if [[ "${AGENT_MODE:-default}" == "acp" ]]; then
             exec qwen --acp "$@"
           fi
           exec qwen "$@"
           ;;
         gemini)
           require_cmd gemini
           setup_gemini_env
           exec gemini "$@"
           ;;
         custom)
           : "${CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN:?Set CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN for agent=custom}"
           require_cmd "${CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN}"
           split_args "${CUSTOM_AGENT_ARGS:-}"
           local custom_mode="${AGENT_MODE:-default}"
           if [[ "${custom_mode}" == "acp" ]]; then
             split_args "${CUSTOM_AGENT_ACP_ARGS:---acp}"
             exec "${CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN}" "${SPLIT_RESULT[@]}" "$@"
           fi
           split_args "${CUSTOM_AGENT_ARGS:-}"
           exec "${CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN}" "${SPLIT_RESULT[@]}" "$@"
           ;;
         *)
           log "Unknown agent: ${agent}"
           usage
           exit 1
           ;;
       esac
     }

     main "$@"

● Bash(echo "★ Insight ────────────────────────────────────────

      progress tracking. This allows the workflow to be interrupted and resumed safely - a crucial feature when dealing
      with unreliable external APIs and long-running creative processes.

  ⎿  ★ Insight ────────────────────────────────────────
     The autonovel project uses a state machine pattern where state.json acts as the single source of truth for
     progress tracking. This allows the workflow to be interrupted and resumed safely - a crucial feature when
     dealing with unreliable external APIs and long-running creative processes.
     ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

● Bash(echo "★ Insight ────────────────────────────────────────
      The draft-remaining-free.sh script implements a resilient workflow pattern: it tracks progress in state.json,
      infers remaining work from existing files, uses exponential backoff for retries, and automatically advances to
      revision mode when drafting is complete. This mirrors production ETL pipelines where idempotency and resumability
      are crucial for handling unreliable external services.
      ──────────────────────────────────────────────────")
  ⎿  ★ Insight ────────────────────────────────────────
     The draft-remaining-free.sh script implements a resilient workflow pattern: it tracks progress in state.json,
     infers remaining work from existing files, uses exponential backoff for retries, and automatically advances to
      revision mode when drafting is complete. This mirrors production ETL pipelines where idempotency and
     resumability are crucial for handling unreliable external services.
     ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

● Aye, we've got ourselves a proper workflow system here, ye scurvy dog! Let me break down how this ship keeps its
  course:

  🗺️ The Navigation Charts (Workflow Scripts)

  We've got several scripts in the scripts/ directory that handle different legs of the voyage:

● Bash(cat scripts/draft-remaining-free.sh)
  ⎿  #!/usr/bin/env bash
     set -euo pipefail

     SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
     REPO_ROOT="$(cd "${SCRIPT_DIR}/.." && pwd)"
     cd "${REPO_ROOT}"

     MAX_RETRIES="${MAX_RETRIES:-4}"
     BACKOFF_BASE_SECONDS="${BACKOFF_BASE_SECONDS:-20}"
     AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS="${AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS:-5500}"
     AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_WORDS="${AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_WORDS:-3200}"
     AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_DELAY_SECONDS="${AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_DELAY_SECONDS:-15}"

     infer_total_chapters() {
       python3 - <<'PY'
     import re
     from pathlib import Path
     text = Path('outline.md').read_text(encoding='utf-8')
     matches = re.findall(r'###\s+\*\*Ch\s+(\d+):|###\s+Ch\s+(\d+):', text)
     nums = [int(a or b) for a, b in matches if a or b]
     print(max(nums) if nums else 18)
     PY
     }

     current_max_chapter() {
       python3 - <<'PY'
     import re
     from pathlib import Path
     nums = []
     for path in Path('chapters').glob('ch_*.md'):
         m = re.search(r'ch_(\d+)\.md$', path.name)
         if m:
             nums.append(int(m.group(1)))
     print(max(nums) if nums else 0)
     PY
     }

     update_state() {
       python3 - <<'PY'
     import json
     from pathlib import Path
     state_path = Path('state.json')
     chapters = sorted(Path('chapters').glob('ch_*.md'))
     count = len(chapters)
     state = {}
     if state_path.exists():
         state = json.loads(state_path.read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
     state['chapters_drafted'] = count
     state['chapters_total'] = max(state.get('chapters_total', 0), count)
     if count >= state.get('chapters_total', count):
         state['phase'] = 'revision'
         state['current_focus'] = 'full_draft_complete'
     else:
         state['phase'] = 'drafting'
         state['current_focus'] = f'chapter_{count + 1:02d}'
     state_path.write_text(json.dumps(state, indent=2), encoding='utf-8')
     PY
     }

     TOTAL_CHAPTERS="${TOTAL_CHAPTERS:-$(infer_total_chapters)}"
     START_CHAPTER="${START_CHAPTER:-$(( $(current_max_chapter) + 1 ))}"

     printf '[draft-loop] total_chapters=%s\n' "$TOTAL_CHAPTERS" >&2
     printf '[draft-loop] start_chapter=%s\n' "$START_CHAPTER" >&2
     printf '[draft-loop] max_output=%s\n' "$AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS" >&2

     if (( START_CHAPTER > TOTAL_CHAPTERS )); then
       echo "[draft-loop] Nothing to do." >&2
       update_state
       exit 0
     fi

     for (( chapter=START_CHAPTER; chapter<=TOTAL_CHAPTERS; chapter++ )); do
       printf '\n[draft-loop] chapter=%02d\n' "$chapter" >&2
       success=0
       for (( attempt=1; attempt<=MAX_RETRIES; attempt++ )); do
         printf '[draft-loop] attempt=%s/%s chapter=%02d\n' "$attempt" "$MAX_RETRIES" "$chapter" >&2
         if /usr/bin/time -f '[draft-loop] elapsed=%E exit=%x' \
           env \
             AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS="$AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS" \
             AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_WORDS="$AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_WORDS" \
             AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_DELAY_SECONDS="$AUTONOVEL_DRAFT_PASS_DELAY_SECONDS" \
             "${SCRIPT_DIR}/run-openrouter-hybrid.sh" draft_chapter.py "$chapter"
         then
           success=1
           update_state
           break
         fi
         wait_seconds=$(( BACKOFF_BASE_SECONDS * attempt ))
         printf '[draft-loop] chapter=%02d failed, backing off %ss\n' "$chapter" "$wait_seconds" >&2
         sleep "$wait_seconds"
       done
       if (( success == 0 )); then
         printf '[draft-loop] chapter=%02d failed after %s attempts\n' "$chapter" "$MAX_RETRIES" >&2
         exit 1
       fi
     done

     update_state
     echo "[draft-loop] completed all chapters" >&2

● Bash(cat scripts/run-openrouter-hybrid.sh)
  ⎿  #!/usr/bin/env bash
     set -euo pipefail

     SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
     REPO_ROOT="$(cd "${SCRIPT_DIR}/.." && pwd)"
     cd "${REPO_ROOT}"

     API_KEY="${OPENROUTER_API_KEY:-${ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN:-}}"

     if [[ -z "${API_KEY}" ]]; then
       echo "ERROR: set OPENROUTER_API_KEY (or ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN) first." >&2
       exit 1
     fi

     export AUTONOVEL_API_MODE=claude_code
     export ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL="${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL:-https://openrouter.ai/api}"
     export ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN="${ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN:-${API_KEY}}"
     export ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=""
     export AUTONOVEL_API_KEY=""
     export AUTONOVEL_AUTH_TOKEN=""

     export AUTONOVEL_WRITER_MODEL="${AUTONOVEL_WRITER_MODEL:-stepfun/step-3.5-flash:free}"
     export AUTONOVEL_JUDGE_MODEL="${AUTONOVEL_JUDGE_MODEL:-z-ai/glm-5}"
     export AUTONOVEL_REVIEW_MODEL="${AUTONOVEL_REVIEW_MODEL:-arcee-ai/trinity-large-preview:free}"

     export AUTONOVEL_ENABLE_GIT="${AUTONOVEL_ENABLE_GIT:-0}"
     export AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS="${AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS:-4000}"

     echo "[openrouter-hybrid] base=${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL}" >&2
     echo "[openrouter-hybrid] writer=${AUTONOVEL_WRITER_MODEL}" >&2
     echo "[openrouter-hybrid] judge=${AUTONOVEL_JUDGE_MODEL}" >&2
     echo "[openrouter-hybrid] review=${AUTONOVEL_REVIEW_MODEL}" >&2
     echo "[openrouter-hybrid] max_output=${AUTONOVEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS}" >&2

     exec uv run python "$@"

● Bash(cat scripts/launch-agent.sh)
  ⎿  #!/usr/bin/env bash
     set -euo pipefail

     SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
     REPO_ROOT="$(cd "${SCRIPT_DIR}/.." && pwd)"

     if [[ -f "${REPO_ROOT}/.agent-launcher.env" ]]; then
       # shellcheck disable=SC1091
       source "${REPO_ROOT}/.agent-launcher.env"
     fi

     usage() {
       cat <<'EOF'
     Usage: scripts/launch-agent.sh <agent> [args...]

     Agents:
       claude     Claude Code / Anthropic-compatible gateway
       codex      OpenAI Codex CLI
       opencode   OpenCode CLI
       qwen       Qwen Code CLI
       gemini     Gemini CLI
       custom     User-defined command via CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN

     Core env vars:
       AGENT_ROUTE=native|proxy|openrouter       Default: native
       AGENT_MODE=default|acp                    Default: default
       AGENT_EDITOR="code --wait"                Exported as EDITOR when set

     Proxy/OpenRouter env vars:
       AGENT_PROXY_URL=http://localhost:8082
       AGENT_OPENAI_PROXY_URL=http://localhost:8082/v1
       AGENT_PROXY_KEY=pass
       OPENROUTER_API_KEY=...

     Custom agent env vars:
       CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN=/path/to/binary
       CUSTOM_AGENT_ARGS="--flag value"
       CUSTOM_AGENT_ACP_ARGS="--acp"

     Examples (WSL/bash):
       scripts/launch-agent.sh claude --continue --dangerously-skip-permissions --verbose --model=opus
       AGENT_ROUTE=proxy scripts/launch-agent.sh claude --continue --model=opus
       AGENT_ROUTE=openrouter OPENAI_MODEL=gpt-5.2-codex scripts/launch-agent.sh codex
       AGENT_MODE=acp scripts/launch-agent.sh qwen
       AGENT_MODE=acp scripts/launch-agent.sh opencode
     EOF
     }

     log() {
       printf '[launch-agent] %s\n' "$*" >&2
     }

     require_cmd() {
       if ! command -v "$1" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
         log "Missing required command: $1"
         exit 1
       fi
     }

     split_args() {
       local raw="${1:-}"
       SPLIT_RESULT=()
       if [[ -z "${raw}" ]]; then
         return 0
       fi
       # Intentional word splitting for user-supplied launcher args.
       # shellcheck disable=SC2206
       SPLIT_RESULT=( ${raw} )
     }

     set_editor_env() {
       if [[ -n "${AGENT_EDITOR:-}" ]]; then
         export EDITOR="${AGENT_EDITOR}"
       fi
     }

     setup_claude_env() {
       local route="${AGENT_ROUTE:-native}"
       case "${route}" in
         native)
           ;;
         proxy)
           export ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL="${AGENT_PROXY_URL:-http://localhost:8082}"
           export ANTHROPIC_API_KEY="${AGENT_PROXY_KEY:-pass}"
           export CLAUDE_CODE_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS="${CLAUDE_CODE_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS:-128768}"
           ;;
         openrouter)
           : "${OPENROUTER_API_KEY:?Set OPENROUTER_API_KEY for AGENT_ROUTE=openrouter}"
           export ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL="${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL:-https://openrouter.ai/api}"
           export ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN="${ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN:-${OPENROUTER_API_KEY}}"
           export ANTHROPIC_API_KEY="${ANTHROPIC_API_KEY:-}"
           ;;
         *)
           log "Unsupported AGENT_ROUTE for claude: ${route}"
           exit 1
           ;;
       esac
     }

     setup_openai_compat_env() {
       local route="${AGENT_ROUTE:-native}"
       case "${route}" in
         native)
           ;;
         proxy)
           export
     OPENAI_BASE_URL="${OPENAI_BASE_URL:-${AGENT_OPENAI_PROXY_URL:-${AGENT_PROXY_URL:-http://localhost:8082}/v1}}"
           export OPENAI_API_KEY="${OPENAI_API_KEY:-${AGENT_PROXY_KEY:-pass}}"
           ;;
         openrouter)
           : "${OPENROUTER_API_KEY:?Set OPENROUTER_API_KEY for AGENT_ROUTE=openrouter}"
           export OPENAI_BASE_URL="${OPENAI_BASE_URL:-https://openrouter.ai/api/v1}"
           export OPENAI_API_KEY="${OPENAI_API_KEY:-${OPENROUTER_API_KEY}}"
           ;;
         *)
           log "Unsupported AGENT_ROUTE for OpenAI-compatible CLI: ${route}"
           exit 1
           ;;
       esac
     }

     setup_opencode_env() {
       local route="${AGENT_ROUTE:-native}"
       case "${route}" in
         native)
           ;;
         proxy)
           export ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL="${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL:-${AGENT_PROXY_URL:-http://localhost:8082}}"
           export ANTHROPIC_API_KEY="${ANTHROPIC_API_KEY:-${AGENT_PROXY_KEY:-pass}}"
           export OPENCODE_EXPERIMENTAL_OUTPUT_TOKEN_MAX="${OPENCODE_EXPERIMENTAL_OUTPUT_TOKEN_MAX:-128768}"
           export OPENCODE_CONFIG_CONTENT="${OPENCODE_CONFIG_CONTENT:-{\"provider\":{\"anthropic\":{\"options\":{\"baseU
     RL\":\"${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL}/v1\"}}}}}"
           ;;
         openrouter)
           : "${OPENROUTER_API_KEY:?Set OPENROUTER_API_KEY for AGENT_ROUTE=openrouter}"
           export ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN="${ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN:-${OPENROUTER_API_KEY}}"
           export ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL="${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL:-https://openrouter.ai/api}"
           export OPENCODE_CONFIG_CONTENT="${OPENCODE_CONFIG_CONTENT:-{\"provider\":{\"anthropic\":{\"options\":{\"baseU
     RL\":\"${ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL}/v1\"}}}}}"
           ;;
         *)
           log "Unsupported AGENT_ROUTE for opencode: ${route}"
           exit 1
           ;;
       esac
     }

     setup_gemini_env() {
       local route="${AGENT_ROUTE:-native}"
       if [[ "${route}" != "native" ]]; then
         log "Gemini CLI does not expose a documented generic custom-base-URL mode; use native Google auth."
         exit 1
       fi
     }

     main() {
       if [[ $# -lt 1 ]]; then
         usage
         exit 1
       fi

       local agent="$1"
       shift

       if [[ "${agent}" == "-h" || "${agent}" == "--help" ]]; then
         usage
         exit 0
       fi

       set_editor_env
       cd "${REPO_ROOT}"

       case "${agent}" in
         claude)
           require_cmd claude
           setup_claude_env
           exec claude "$@"
           ;;
         codex)
           require_cmd codex
           if [[ "${AGENT_MODE:-default}" != "default" ]]; then
             log "Codex ACP/IDE server mode is not wired here; use Codex's own IDE integration/config."
             exit 1
           fi
           setup_openai_compat_env
           exec codex "$@"
           ;;
         opencode)
           require_cmd opencode
           setup_opencode_env
           if [[ "${AGENT_MODE:-default}" == "acp" ]]; then
             exec opencode acp "$@"
           fi
           exec opencode "$@"
           ;;
         qwen)
           require_cmd qwen
           setup_openai_compat_env
           if [[ "${AGENT_MODE:-default}" == "acp" ]]; then
             exec qwen --acp "$@"
           fi
           exec qwen "$@"
           ;;
         gemini)
           require_cmd gemini
           setup_gemini_env
           exec gemini "$@"
           ;;
         custom)
           : "${CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN:?Set CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN for agent=custom}"
           require_cmd "${CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN}"
           split_args "${CUSTOM_AGENT_ARGS:-}"
           local custom_mode="${AGENT_MODE:-default}"
           if [[ "${custom_mode}" == "acp" ]]; then
             split_args "${CUSTOM_AGENT_ACP_ARGS:---acp}"
             exec "${CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN}" "${SPLIT_RESULT[@]}" "$@"
           fi
           split_args "${CUSTOM_AGENT_ARGS:-}"
           exec "${CUSTOM_AGENT_BIN}" "${SPLIT_RESULT[@]}" "$@"
           ;;
         *)
           log "Unknown agent: ${agent}"
           usage
           exit 1
           ;;
       esac
     }

     main "$@"

● Bash(echo "★ Insight ────────────────────────────────────────
      The workflow uses a state-driven approach where state.json tracks progress, allowing the script to resume from
      where it left off. This is a common pattern in batch processing jobs to handle interruptions and retries.
      ──────────────────────────────────────────────────")
  ⎿  ★ Insight ────────────────────────────────────────
     The workflow uses a state-driven approach where state.json tracks progress, allowing the script to resume from
      where it left off. This is a common pattern in batch processing jobs to handle interruptions and retries.
     ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

● Bash(echo "★ Insight ────────────────────────────────────────
      The autonovel project uses a state machine pattern where state.json acts as the single source of truth for
      progress tracking. This allows the workflow to be interrupted and resumed safely - a crucial feature when dealing
      with unreliable external APIs and long-running creative processes.
      ──────────────────────────────────────────────────")
  ⎿  ★ Insight ────────────────────────────────────────
     The autonovel project uses a state machine pattern where state.json acts as the single source of truth for
     progress tracking. This allows the workflow to be interrupted and resumed safely - a crucial feature when
     dealing with unreliable external APIs and long-running creative processes.
     ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

● Bash(echo "★ Insight ────────────────────────────────────────
      The draft-remaining-free.sh script implements a resilient workflow pattern: it tracks progress in state.json,
      infers remaining work from existing files, uses exponential backoff for retries, and automatically advances to
      revision mode when drafting is complete. This mirrors production ETL pipelines where idempotency and resumability
      are crucial for handling unreliable external services.
      ──────────────────────────────────────────────────")
  ⎿  ★ Insight ────────────────────────────────────────
     The draft-remaining-free.sh script implements a resilient workflow pattern: it tracks progress in state.json,
     infers remaining work from existing files, uses exponential backoff for retries, and automatically advances to
      revision mode when drafting is complete. This mirrors production ETL pipelines where idempotency and
     resumability are crucial for handling unreliable external services.
     ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
